<script type="text/javascript">
	in_popup = false;
	in_hover = false;
	shown = {};
	$(function(){
		$('a.summary, div.premiumText').hover(function(e){
			var is_chrome = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().indexOf('chrome') > -1;
			var is_safari = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().indexOf('safari') > -1;
			var is_ipad = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().indexOf('ipad') > -1;
			in_popup = false;
			in_hover = true;
			var offerbox=document.getElementById("summarytip");
			offerbox.style.visibility = "hidden";
			/*if( is_chrome || (is_safari && is_ipad) )
				var docele = document.body;
			else
				var docele = document.documentElement;*/
			if( is_ipad || is_chrome || is_safari )
				var docele = document.body?document.body:document.documentElement;
			else
				var docele = document.documentElement?document.documentElement:document.body;
			var base_scroll_height = docele.scrollHeight;
			load_tip($(this).attr("rel"), $(this));
			offerbox.style.left=docele.scrollLeft+e.clientX+5+'px';
			if( $(this).hasClass('premiumText') )
			{
				var link = $('div.page');
				var position = link.position();
				var right = $(window).width() - position.left - link.width();
                var mx = e.pageX - $('div.page').offset().left;
				if( (mx+450) > $('div.page').width() )
                    offerbox.style.left=docele.scrollLeft+e.clientX+5-(mx+450-$('div.page').width())+'px';
			}
			if(docele.scrollTop+e.clientY-offerbox.offsetHeight-3 >= 0){
				offerbox.style.top=docele.scrollTop+e.clientY-offerbox.offsetHeight+6+'px';
			} else {offerbox.style.top = '0px';}
			if(offerbox.offsetTop < docele.scrollTop) offerbox.style.top = docele.scrollTop+'px';
			if(docele.scrollHeight > base_scroll_height || (offerbox.offsetTop+offerbox.offsetHeight) > docele.scrollHeight){
				offerbox.style.top=base_scroll_height-offerbox.offsetHeight+'px';
			}
			offerbox.style.visibility="visible";
			load_photo($(this).attr("rel"));
			return true;
		},
		function(){
			in_hover = false;
			setTimeout(function(){
				if( in_popup || in_hover )
					return false;
				var offerbox=document.getElementById("summarytip");
				offerbox.style.visibility = "hidden";
				in_hover = false;
				in_popup = false;
				return true;
			}, 2000);
		});
		$('div#summarytip').hover(function(){
			in_popup = true;
		},
		function(){$(this).css('visibility', 'hidden');in_popup=false;return false;}
		);

		$("#popup_note").click(function() {
			var a = $(this);
			$.getJSON("/form" + a.attr("href"), function(data) {
				if (data.status === "ok") {
					if (data.message['stored'])
					{
						$('a.summary[rel="' + a.attr('rel') + '"], div.premiumText[rel="' + a.attr('rel') + '"]').addClass('innote');
						a.text('Убрать из блокнота');
					}
					else
					{
						$('a.summary[rel="' + a.attr('rel') + '"], div.premiumText[rel="' + a.attr('rel') + '"]').removeClass('innote');
						a.text('В блокнот');
					}
					// показываем общее число объявлений в блокноте
					if (data.message['count'] > 0) {
						$(".my-notebook").show().find(".noted").text(data.message['info']);
					} else {
						$(".my-notebook").hide();
					}
				} else {
					alert(data.message);
				}
			});
			return false;
		});

		$("#popup_cont_trigger").bind('click', function(){
			var a = $(this);
			var id = realhref($(this));
			$.getJSON("/form/user/addvisit/" + id, function(data) {
				if (data.status === "ok") {
					$('a.summary[rel="' + id + '"], div.premiumText[rel="' + id + '"]').addClass('shown');
					if( typeof cc_098_wmvf7 == 'function' )
                        cc_098_wmvf7(offer_data[id]['catalog']);
				}
			});
			a.hide().next().show();
			return false;
		});
	});

	function realhref(item) {
		/* IE 6-7 fix */
		if ($.browser.msie && $.browser.version.substr(0,1)<8)
		{
			var href = item.attr("href");
			return href.substring(href.indexOf('#')).substr(1);
		}
		/*************/
		return item.attr("href").substr(1);
	}

	function load_tip(i, a)
	{
		$('#popup_url').attr("href", "/ru/offer/"+i);
		$('#popup_profile').attr("href", "/ru/profile/"+offer_data[i]['profile']);
		$('#popup_summary').html(offer_data[i]['summary']);
		$('#popup_note').attr("href", "/user/notebook/toggle/" + i);
		$('#popup_note').attr("rel", i);
		$('#popup_sms').attr("href", "/ru/smsup/"+i);
		$('#popup_chart').attr("href", "/ru/offerchart_1/"+i);
		if( a.hasClass('innote') )
			$('#popup_note').text('Убрать из блокнота');
		else
			$('#popup_note').text('В блокнот');
		if( offer_data[i]['details'] )
			$('#p_popup_details').show().next('#popup_details').html(offer_data[i]['details']);
		else
			$('#p_popup_details').hide().next('#popup_details').html('');
		if( offer_data[i]['price'].length )
			$('#popup_price').show().next().show().html(offer_data[i]['price']);
		else
			$('#popup_price').hide().next().hide();
		if( offer_data[i]['contacts'] )
		{
			if( a.hasClass('shown') )
			{
				$("#popup_cont_trigger").hide().next().show();
			}
			else
			{
				$("#popup_cont_trigger").show().next().hide();
				$("#popup_cont_trigger").attr('href', '#' + i);
			}
			$("#popup_contacts").show();
			$("#popup_conttext").html('');
			for( con in offer_data[i]['contacts'] )
			{
				if( offer_data[i]['contacts'][con]['type'] == 'co' )
                    $("#popup_conttext").append('<div class="icon item" style="background-image: url(\'http://torg.uz/image/contact/1.gif\');"><img src="http://torg.uz/contact.php?xf=' + offer_data[i]['contacts'][con]['number'] + '&xc=co"/></div>');
				else
					$("#popup_conttext").append('<div class="icon item" style="background-image: url(\'http://torg.uz/image/contact/' + offer_data[i]['contacts'][con]['type'] + '.gif\');">' + offer_data[i]['contacts'][con]['number'] + '</div>');
			}
		}
		else
		{
			$("#popup_cont_trigger").hide();
			$("#popup_contacts").hide();
		}
	}

	function load_photo(i)
	{
    var par = $('#fb_photo');
    var child = $('#fb_photo').children('img');

		$('#fb_photo').attr("href", '#').children('img').attr("src", 'http://torg.uz/image/nophoto.gif');
		if( offer_data[i]['photo'].length )
		{
			child.hide();
			par.attr("href", 'http://torg.uz/image/offer/' + offer_data[i]['photo'] + '_b.jpg');
			child.attr("src", 'http://torg.uz/image/offer/' + offer_data[i]['photo'] + '_s.jpg');
			child.load(function(){
			$(this).show();
			});
		}
	}
</script>

			<a href="#" id="showfilter" class="showfilter">Развернуть фильтр</a>
		</div>
				<script type="text/javascript">
			var field_value = {};
			$(document).ready(function(){
				var regionfilter = new fancyselect("regionfilter", true);
				var vendors = new fancyselect("vendors", true);
				var models = new fancyselect("models", true);
				$('a.regionfilter').parents('div.parameter').addClass('filternote');
				$('a.regionfilter').parents('div.parameter').children('div.caption').css('font-size', '14px');
							check_filter();
				$("div.filter > form").bind('submit', function(){
					if( ($('input[name="price[min]"]').val() || $('input[name="price[max]"]').val()) && $('select[name="price[currency]"]').val() == 0 )
					{
						alert('Укажите валюту!');
						return false;
					}
				});
				$("#showfilter").bind('click', function(){
					$("div.hidden_filter").toggle();
					if( $("div.hidden_filter").css('display') == 'block' )
						$(this).text('Свернуть фильтр');
					else
						$(this).text('Развернуть фильтр');
					return false;
				});
				function check_filter()
				{
					var count = 0;
					$("div.filter > form").find('input[checked="checked"], input[type="text"]').each(function(){
						if( $(this).val() )
						{
							$(this).parents('div.field').show();
							count++;
						}
					});
					if( count )
					{
						$("div.hidden_filter").show();
						$("a.showfilter").text('Свернуть фильтр');
					}
				}
				function recheck()
				{
					var value = [];
					if( $('a.vendors').length )
					{
						vendors.values().each(function() {
							var id = $(this).val();
							value.push(id);
						});
						$('.models').attr('href', $('.models').attr('href') +'/' + value.join(","));
					}
				}
				recheck();
				vendors.afterSelect = function(data) {
					if (models.name != undefined) {
						var value = { "id": [], "title": [], "parent": [] };
						models.href("/models/" + data["id"].join(","));
						models.value.find("input." + data["id"].join(",input.")).each(function() {
							var item = $(this);
							value["id"].push(item.val());
							value["title"].push(item.attr("title"));
							value["parent"].push(item.attr("class"));
						});
						models.set(value);
					}
				}

				models.summary = function() {
					var data = [];
					var value = [];
					models.values().each(function() {
						var parent = $(this).attr("class");
						if (data[parent] == undefined) {
							data[parent] = [];
						}
						data[parent].push($(this).attr("title"));
					});
					vendors.values().each(function() {
						var id = $(this).val();
						var title = $(this).attr("title");
						if (data[id] != undefined) {
							title += " (" + data[id].join(", ") + ")";
						}
						value.push(title);
					});
					return value.join(", ");
				}
						});
		</script>
		<div class="buttons">
			<button type="submit">Применить</button>
		</div>
	</form>
